## Sichuan Events ##
## By Alpinia     ##

add_namespace = sichuan
add_namespace = NKRsichuan
add_namespace = NKRsichuanmisc

### System Events ###

country_event = { #fire new CIFRC events
	id = sichuan.1000
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SZC_major_famine }
	}

	immediate = {
		#Weekly loop
		country_event = { id = sichuan.1000 days = 4 random_hours = 144 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1000 option 1"
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { SZC.SZC_famine_PP = 30 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1000 option 2"
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { SZC.SZC_famine_PP = 20 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1000 option 3"
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { SZC.SZC_famine_PP = 10 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1000 option 4"
		ai_chance = { base = 4 }
		add_to_variable = { SZC.SZC_famine_PP = 5 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1000 option 5"
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}
}

country_event = { #fire opium events
	id = sichuan.1001
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_opium_crisis_solved }
		SZC_opium_corruption_active = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		#Monthly loop
		country_event = { id = sichuan.1001 days = 20 random_hours = 240 }
	}

	option = { #Civil Service Corruption
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 1"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_civil_corruption_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_civil_corruption_event
		country_event = sichuan.208
	}

	option = { #Army Corruption
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 2"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_army_corruption_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_army_corruption_event
		country_event = sichuan.209
	}

	option = { #Smugglers in the Administration
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 3"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_smugglers_administration_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_smugglers_administration_event
		country_event = sichuan.210
	}

	option = { #Smugglers in the Administration
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 4"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_opium_corruption_event }
			has_country_flag = SZC_civil_corruption_event
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_army_corruption_event
				has_country_flag = SZC_smugglers_administration_event
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_opium_corruption_event
		country_event = sichuan.211
	}

	option = { #Political Murders
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 5"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_assassinations_event }
			OR = {
				has_idea = SZC_opium_corruption_3
				has_idea = SZC_opium_corruption_4
				has_idea = SZC_opium_corruption_5
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_assassinations_event
		country_event = sichuan.212
	}

	option = { #Tax Evasion Discovered
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 6"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SZC_monopoly_path
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_first_tax_evasion_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_first_tax_evasion_event
		country_event = sichuan.215
	}

	option = { #Extensive Tax Evasion
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 7"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SZC_monopoly_path
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_second_tax_evasion_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_second_tax_evasion_event
		country_event = sichuan.216
	}

	option = { #Merchants Revolt Against Monopoly
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 8"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SZC_monopoly_path
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_merchant_resistance_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_merchant_resistance_event
		country_event = sichuan.217
	}

	option = { #Illegal Production Continues to Increase
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 9"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SZC_monopoly_path
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_illegal_production_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_illegal_production_event
		country_event = sichuan.219
	}

	option = { #generic corruption events
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 10"
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
		random_list = {
			20 = { set_country_flag = { flag = SZC_corruption_event_delays days = 2 value = 1 } }
			20 = { set_country_flag = { flag = SZC_corruption_event_bribes days = 2 value = 1 } }
			20 = { set_country_flag = { flag = SZC_corruption_event_no_enforcement days = 2 value = 1 } }
		}
		country_event = sichuan.206
	}

	option = { #generic corruption event
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 11"
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
		country_event = sichuan.221
	}

	option = { #nothing
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1001 option 12"
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
	}
}

country_event = { #fire famine flavour events
	id = sichuan.1002
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SZC_major_famine }
	}

	immediate = {
		#Monthly loop
		country_event = { id = sichuan.1002 days = 21 random_hours = 168 }
	}

	option = { #Dujiangyan, Damaged
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1002 option 1"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SZC_baopingkou_flooded
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_dujiangyan_damaged_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 9000 }
		clr_country_flag = SZC_baopingkou_flooded
		set_country_flag = SZC_dujiangyan_damaged_event
		country_event = sichuan.175
	}

	option = { #Y.C. James Yen's Donation
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1002 option 2"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_james_yen_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_james_yen_event
		country_event = sichuan.176
	}

	option = { #The Clay Eaters

		country_event = sichuan.170
	}

	option = { #Corruption Delays Relief Efforts
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1002 option 10"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SZC_first_corruption_event
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_corruption_event }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = SZC_corruption_event days = 32 value = 1 }
		country_event = sichuan.171
	}

	option = { #Black Market on Foodstuffs
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1002 option 11"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_black_market_event }

		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
		set_country_flag = SZC_black_market_event
		country_event = sichuan.172
	}

	option = { #Left KMT Raids Food Shipments
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1002 option 12"
		trigger = {
			country_exists = CHI
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SZC_left_kmt_raids_event
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_government = social_liberal
			}

		country_event = sichuan.174

	option = { #none
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1002 option 14"
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to move remnants
	id = sichuan.1003
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		SZC_zhili_in_exile = yes
		XXA = { any_character = { has_character_flag = QIE_zhili_leader } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1003 option 1"
		XXA = {
			random_character = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = QIE_zhili_leader }
				set_nationality = SZC
				unit_leader_event = sichuan.273
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = sichuan.1003 days = 10 random_hours = 240 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = sichuan.1005

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1005 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = QIE
				QIE = {
					china_is_aligned_with_zhili = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_armament }
				}
			}
			QIE = { country_event = sichuan.16 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = ANQ
				ANQ = {
					china_is_aligned_with_zhili = yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_armament }
				}
			}
			ANQ = { country_event = sichuan.16 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = LEP
				LEP = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_armament }
				}
			}
			LEP = { country_event = sichuan.16 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = sichuan.1006

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1006 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = YUN
				YUN = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = SZC_refused_baoding
						has_idea = YUN_chaos_army
					}
				}
			}
			YUN = { country_event = sichuan.17 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CHI
				CHI = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_baoding }
				}
			}
			CHI = { country_event = sichuan.17 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = FNG
				FNG = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_baoding }
				}
			}
			FNG = { country_event = sichuan.17 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = sichuan.1007

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1007 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = GXC
					exists = yes
					GXC_has_guangxi_government = yes
					china_is_aligned_with_zhili = no
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_xiang }
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = GXC
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					GXC_has_guangxi_government = yes
					china_is_aligned_with_zhili = no
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_xiang }
				}
				country_event = sichuan.18
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = ANQ
				ANQ = {
					china_is_aligned_with_zhili = no
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_xiang }
				}
			}
			ANQ = { country_event = sichuan.18 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = FNG
				FNG = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_xiang }
				}
			}
			FNG = { country_event = sichuan.18 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = sichuan.1008

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.1008 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = GXC
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						GXC_has_federalist_government = yes
						GXC_has_KMT_government = yes
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_officers }
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = GXC
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						GXC_has_federalist_government = yes
						GXC_has_KMT_government = yes
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_officers }
				}
				country_event = sichuan.19
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CHI
				CHI = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_refused_officers }
				}
			}
			CHI = { country_event = sichuan.19 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = YUN
				YUN = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = SZC_refused_officers
						has_country_leader = { character = YUN_long_yun }
					}
				}
			}
			YUN = { country_event = sichuan.19 }
		}
	}
}

	id = sichuan.5
	title = sichuan.5.t
	desc = sichuan.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_yang_sen_field_3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.5 option sichuan.5.a"
		name = sichuan.5.a
		add_stability = -0.02
	}
}

country_event = { #Chaos in the South (triggered by QIE)
	id = sichuan.7
	title = sichuan.7.t

	desc = {
		text = sichuan.7.d.intervention
		trigger = {
			QIE = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = wu_intervenes_proLEP
					has_country_flag = wu_intervenes_proANQ
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = sichuan.7.d.no_intervention
		trigger = {
			QIE = {
				has_country_flag = wu_no_intervene
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_cao_kun_4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.7 option sichuan.7.a"
		name = sichuan.7.a
		add_stability = -0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = sichuan.8 days = 2 random_hours = 24 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Liu Xiang Mobilises Against Us
	id = sichuan.8
	title = sichuan.8.t
	desc = sichuan.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_liu_xiang

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.8 option sichuan.8.a"
		name = sichuan.8.a
		add_stability = -0.03
		650 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			delete_units = { division_template = "Shiye Tuan Bubing Shi" disband = yes }
			delete_units = { division_template = "Shiye Tuan Jingying Shi" disband = yes }
		}
		else = {
			delete_units = { division_template = "Shiye Tuan Bubing Shi" }
			delete_units = { division_template = "Shiye Tuan Jingying Shi" }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = sichuan.9 days = 1 random_hours = 28 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #War in Sichuan
	id = sichuan.9
	title = sichuan.9.t
	desc = sichuan.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_yang_sen_field_4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.9 option sichuan.9.a"
		name = sichuan.9.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = QIE_manchu_restoration } }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SZC_internal_divisions
			add_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea
		}
		QIE = { country_event = sichuan.50 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		effect_tooltip = { every_country_division = { custom_effect_tooltip = will_be_disbanded } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				delete_unit = { disband = yes }
			}
			else = {
				delete_unit = { disband = no }
			}

			set_country_flag = { flag = SZC_armament_defeats value = 0 }

			#Officer Support
			YUN = { country_event = { id = sichuan.53 days = 2 } }

			#Battles
			QIE = { country_event = { id = sichuan.101 days = 4 } }
			country_event = { id = sichuan.55 days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = sichuan.59 days = 18 }
			country_event = { id = sichuan.63 days = 28 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.9 option sichuan.9.b"
		name = sichuan.9.b
		trigger = { has_global_flag = QIE_manchu_restoration }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SZC_internal_divisions
			add_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				delete_unit = { disband = yes }
			}
			else = {
				delete_unit = { disband = no }
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = SZC_armament_defeats value = 0 }

			#QIE informed
			QIE = { country_event = { id = qiefor.108 hours = 8 } }

			#Officer Support
			YUN = { country_event = { id = sichuan.53 days = 2 } }

			#Battles
			QIE = { country_event = { id = sichuan.101 days = 4 } }
			country_event = { id = sichuan.55 days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = sichuan.59 days = 18 }
			country_event = { id = sichuan.63 days = 28 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Neijiang Under Assault
	id = sichuan.59
	title = sichuan.59.t
	desc = sichuan.59.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_militia

	trigger = {
		has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea
		has_government = authoritarian_democrat
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.59 option sichuan.59.a"
		name = sichuan.59.a #defend the bridgeheads
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity@social_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity@social_liberal
			}
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity@paternal_autocrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_YANG_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_LIU_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_ZHL_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_ZHL_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_SOCLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SZC_battle_neijiang_defend
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = sichuan.60 days = 3 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.59 option sichuan.59.b"
		name = sichuan.59.b #blow the bridges
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity@market_liberal
			}
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity@social_conservative
			}
			modifier = {
				add = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_MARLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SZC_battle_neijiang_blow
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = sichuan.61 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Deng Xihou Takes Chengdu
	id = sichuan.62
	title = sichuan.62.t
	desc = sichuan.62.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_deng_xihou

	trigger = {
		has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea
		has_government = authoritarian_democrat
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.62 option sichuan.62.a"
		name = sichuan.62.a
		remove_ideas = SZC_baoding_influence
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		clr_country_flag = SZC_armament_defeats
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Wubei Xi Bubing Shi" }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_political_party = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0 }
			SZC_armament_department_flees = yes
			load_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Baoding
		}
		SZC_deng_xihou = { promote_leader = yes }
	}
}

country_event = { #The Siege of Chengdu
	id = sichuan.63
	title = sichuan.63.t
	desc = sichuan.63.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_riot

	trigger = {
		has_idea = SZC_civil_war_idea
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
				country_event = { id = sichuan.64 days = 3 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = sichuan.82 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.63 option sichuan.63.a"
		name = sichuan.63.a
		army_experience = 5
	}
}

country_event = { #Governor Xiao invades Enshi (SZC)
	id = sichuan.102
	title = sichuan.102.t
	desc = sichuan.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_federalist_troops_march

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Liu Xiang manages to fend them off
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.102 option sichuan.102.a"
		name = sichuan.102.a
		ai_chance = { base = 70 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				add_political_power = -10
				add_manpower = -3000
			}
			else = {
				SZC_baoding_defeat = yes
			}
			QIE = { country_event = { id = sichuan.104 days = 5 } }
		}
	}

	option = { #Liu Xiang is defeated!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.102 option sichuan.102.b"
		name = sichuan.102.b
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			SZC_armament_victory = yes
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		else = {
			SZC_baoding_victory = yes
			add_political_power = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			1049 = {
				remove_claim_by = SZC
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			QIE = { country_event = { id = sichuan.103 days = 5 } }
		}
	}
}

			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Labour_Relief target = THIS }

			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Enact_Price_Controls target = THIS }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Increase_Relief_Efforts target = THIS }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Food_Banks target = THIS }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Subsidise_Food_Production target = THIS }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_International_Famine_Relief target = THIS }

			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Request_Aid target = QIE }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Request_Aid target = FNG }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Request_Aid target = GXC }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Request_Aid target = LEC }

			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Import_Grain target = GEA }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Import_Grain target = GXC }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Import_Grain target = AST }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = SZC_Import_Grain target = CAN }

			set_variable = { SZC_famine_monthly_population = -2 }
			set_variable = { SZC_famine_stability_factor = -0.25 }
			set_variable = { SZC_famine_war_support_factor = -1 }
			set_variable = { SZC_famine_consumer_goods_factor = 0.5 }

			country_event = { id = sichuan.1002 days = 20 random_hours = 144 }

			news_event = { id = sichuan.124 days = 5 random_hours = 48 }
		}

	id = sichuan.200
	title = sichuan.200.t
	desc = sichuan.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_china_opium_field_1

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = SZC_opium_crisis_solved }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.200 option sichuan.200.a"
		name = sichuan.200.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			#Xiang is pro-opium
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Industrial
			}
			#Armament is pro-opium
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Armament
			}
			#Military Zhili are pro-opium
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = SZC_the_return_of_tianjin
			}
			#Tian Songyao/Liu Wenhui favour opium
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { SZC_opium_removal_desire_tian = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
				multiply_temp_variable = { SZC_opium_removal_desire_tian = -10 }
				add = SZC_opium_removal_desire_tian

				has_focus_tree = Sichuan_Clique_Baoding
				has_character = SZC_tian_songyao
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { SZC_opium_removal_desire_liu = party_popularity@market_liberal }
				multiply_temp_variable = { SZC_opium_removal_desire_liu = -10 }
				add = SZC_opium_removal_desire_liu

		}

			base = 10
			#Armament is pro-opium

		}

country_event = { #Fall of the Manchu
	id = sichuan.277
	title = sichuan.277.t
	desc = sichuan.277.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_puyi_wanrong_couple

	trigger = {
		SZC_zhili_in_exile = yes
		owns_state = 608
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.277 option sichuan.277.a"
		name = sichuan.277.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = QIE_guo_jijiao }
			QIE_guo_jijiao = {
				add_max_trait = 1
				add_timed_unit_leader_trait = {
					trait = wounded
					days = 60
				}
				gain_xp = 25
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = SZC_vindicating_the_invisible_element_idea
			set_country_flag = SZC_zhili_conquer_QIE_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			QIE = {
				QIE_zhang_guotao = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
					promote_character = totalist_subtype
				}
				QIE_li_dazhao = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
					promote_character = syndicalist_subtype
				}
				QIE_liu_kanyuan = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
					promote_character = radical_socialist_subtype
				}
				QIE_liu_chongyou = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
					promote_character = social_democrat_subtype
				}
				QIE_xu_qin = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
						promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								desc = QIE_xu_qin_leader_desc
								ideology = social_conservative_subtype
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				QIE_zeng_qi = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
					promote_character = national_populist_subtype
				}
			}
			QIE_hu_shih = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
					promote_character = social_liberal_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = QIE_hu_shih_leader_desc
							ideology = social_liberal_subtype
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			QIE_huang_fu = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
					promote_character = market_liberal_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = QIE_huang_fu_leader_desc
							ideology = market_liberal_subtype
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				name = QIE_totalist_party
				long_name = QIE_totalist_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				name = QIE_syndicalist_party
				long_name = QIE_syndicalist_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				name = QIE_radical_socialist_party
				long_name = QIE_radical_socialist_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				name = QIE_all_chinese_national_salvation_congress_party
				long_name = QIE_all_chinese_national_salvation_congress_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				name = QIE_social_liberal_party
				long_name = QIE_social_liberal_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				name = QIE_Old_PSC_party
				long_name = QIE_Old_PSC_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				name = QIE_democratic_constitutionalist_party
				long_name = QIE_democratic_constitutionalist_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {

			}

country_event = { #Culmination of the Great Struggle
	id = sichuan.282
	title = sichuan.282.t
	desc = sichuan.282.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_hu_shih_yan_huiqing

	trigger = {
		SZC_zhili_in_exile = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SZC_zhili_held_elections_flag
			add_advisor_role = {
				character = QIE_yan_huiqing
				advisor = {
					slot = second_in_command
					idea_token = QIE_yan_huiqing_sic
					desc = QIE_yan_huiqing_advisor_desc
					traits = { KR_gentleman_polymath_sic }
					can_be_fired = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.282 option sichuan.282.a"
		name = sichuan.282.a #Gao sweeps the Assembly!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SZC_path option = SZC_PATH_ZHL_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE_gao_lingwei = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
					promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = QIE_gao_lingwei_leader_desc
							ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_trait = QIE_squire_of_tianjin } }
					add_trait = { trait = QIE_squire_of_tianjin ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					QIE_wang_chengbin = {
						NOT = { has_trait = KR_marshal_of_tianjin }
					}
				}
				QIE_wang_chengbin = {
					remove_army_chief_role = yes
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = army_chief
							idea_token = QIE_wang_chengbin_army_chief
							traits = { KR_marshal_of_tianjin }
							cost = 200
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					QIE_yan_huiqing = {
						NOT = { is_second_in_command = yes }
					}
				}
				activate_advisor = QIE_yan_huiqing_sic
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.282 option sichuan.282.b"
		name = sichuan.282.b #The Diplomat's honeyed words win the day!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_completed_focus = SZC_the_path_of_reform
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE_yan_huiqing = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
					promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = QIE_yan_huiqing_leader_desc
							ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_trait = QIE_the_diplomat
							has_trait = QIE_the_diplomat_2
						}
					}
					add_trait = { trait = QIE_the_diplomat ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					QIE_wang_chengbin = {
						NOT = { has_trait = KR_marshal_of_tianjin }
					}
				}
				QIE_wang_chengbin = {
					remove_army_chief_role = yes
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = army_chief
							idea_token = QIE_wang_chengbin_army_chief
							traits = { KR_marshal_of_tianjin }
							cost = 200
						}
					}
				}
			}
			activate_advisor = QIE_gao_lingwei_sic
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Diarchy/Returning Control
	id = sichuan.352
	title = sichuan.352.t
	desc = sichuan.352.d

	trigger = {
		SZC_has_baoding_government = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.352 option sichuan.352.a"
		name = sichuan.352.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				name = SZC_Gang_Of_Nine_party
				long_name = SZC_Gang_Of_Nine_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				name = SZC_Liu_Clique_party
				long_name = SZC_Liu_Clique_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				name = SZC_Deng_Clique_party
				long_name = SZC_Deng_Clique_party_long
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = SZC_tian_songyao }
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					name = SZC_Tian_Clique_party
					long_name = SZC_Tian_Clique_party_long
				}
				SZC_tian_songyao = {
					remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = SZC_tian_songyao_leader_desc
							ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			add_ideas = SZC_diarchy_wenhui_2
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = SZC_diarchy_neutral
		}
	}
}

					}
				}

					prioritize_location = 10726
					owner = ROOT
				}

country_event = { #Chen Jiongming Arrives in Sichuan
	id = sichuan.511
	title = sichuan.511.t
	desc = sichuan.511.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_chen_jiongming

	trigger = {
		is_subject = no
		has_elected_government = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sichuan.511 option sichuan.511.a"
		name = sichuan.511.a
		add_political_power = 200
		GXC_move_federalist_generals = yes
		event_target:original_liangguang = {
			GXC_chen_jiongming = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
					promote_character = social_liberal_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = GXC_chen_jiongming_leader_desc
							ideology = social_liberal_subtype
							traits = { CHN_federalist_aligned }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = social_democrat_subtype }
					promote_character = social_democrat_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = GXC_chen_jiongming_leader_desc
							ideology = social_democrat_subtype
							traits = { CHN_federalist_aligned }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes

				SZC_diarchy_wenhui_3

				SZC_social_welfare_7
				SZC_social_welfare_8
				SZC_social_welfare_9
				SZC_social_welfare_10
				SZC_social_welfare_11
				SZC_social_welfare_12
				SZC_social_welfare_13
				SZC_social_welfare_14
				SZC_social_welfare_15
				SZC_social_welfare_16
				SZC_social_welfare_17
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SZC_Restructure_The_Army }
				set_country_flag = SZC_Restructure_The_Army_completed
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SZC_Recruit_NRA_Veterans }
				set_country_flag = SZC_Recruit_NRA_Veterans_completed
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SZC_Form_Minjun }
				set_country_flag = SZC_Form_Minjun_completed
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SZC_The_Sichuan_Provincial_Army }
				set_country_flag = SZC_The_Sichuan_Provincial_Army_completed
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SZC_Military_Affairs_Commission }
				set_country_flag = SZC_Military_Affairs_Commission_completed
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SZC_The_Guofangjun_Model }
				set_country_flag = SZC_The_Guofangjun_Model_completed
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SZC_Civil_Service_Reform }
				set_country_flag = SZC_Civil_Service_Reform_completed
			}
			if = {

			}
			if = {

				set_country_flag = SZC_Judicial_Renewal_completed
			}
			load_focus_tree = {
				tree = Sichuan_Clique_Federalist
				keep_completed = yes

			}

country_event = { #
	id = NKRsichuan.104
	title = NKRsichuan.104.t
	desc = NKRsichuan.104.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_chen_gongbo_speech_2

	trigger = {
		original_tag = SZC
		has_country_flag = NKRSZCpanpath
		is_subject_of = LKT
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SZC_pan_declare_southernwest_autonomy
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {#
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuan.104 option NKRsichuan.104.a"
		name = NKRsichuan.104.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_focus_tree_will_change_tt
		SZC_pan_wenhua = {
			set_variable = {
				china_alignment = token:left_kuomintang
			}
			country_leader = {
				swap_country_leader_traits = {
					remove = CHN_non_aligned
					add = CHN_left_kuomintang_aligned
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_country_flag = NKRSZC_joinkmt
		complete_national_focus = SZC_pan_a_red_sichuan
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SZC_pan_legitimacy_3
			add_idea = SZC_pan_legitimacy_4
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = NKRsichuan.106
				days = 7
			}
			country_event = {
				id =  NKRsichuan.108
				days = 14
			}
			SZC_liu_bocheng = {
				unit_leader_event = {
					id = NKRsichuanmisc.3
					days = 10
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 17
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = 17
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 5
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 5
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 5
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = SZC_Pan_LKMT_party_long
				name = SZC_Pan_LKMT_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = SZC_Pan_LKMT_party_long
				name = SZC_Pan_LKMT_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = SZC_CRS_party_long
				name = SZC_CRS_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = SZC_KMTPAC_party_long
				name = SZC_KMTPAC_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = SZC_KMTRCA_party_long
				name = SZC_KMTRCA_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = SZC_officer_clique_party_long
				name = SZC_officer_clique_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = SZC_KMTRCF_party_long
				name = SZC_KMTRCF_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = SZC_KMTPSC_party_long
				name = SZC_KMTPSC_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = SZC_KMTWHC_party_long
				name = SZC_KMTWHC_party
			}
			SZC_assorted_leaders = {
				promote_character = totalist_subtype
				promote_character = radical_socialist_subtype
				promote_character = syndicalist_subtype
				promote_character = social_liberal_subtype
				promote_character = market_liberal_subtype
				promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
			}
			SZC_pan_wenhua = {
				promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				country_leader = {
					swap_country_leader_traits = {
						remove = CHN_non_aligned
						add = CHN_left_kuomintang_aligned
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}

######

unit_leader_event = {
	id = NKRsichuanmisc.1 #
	title = {
		text = NKRsichuanmisc.1.t.SZC_pan_wenhua
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_pan_wenhua } }
	}
	title = {
		text = NKRsichuanmisc.1.t.SZC_tang_shizun
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_tang_shizun } }
	}
	title = {
		text = NKRsichuanmisc.1.t.SZC_fan_shaozeng
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_fan_shaozeng } }
	}
	title = {
		text = NKRsichuanmisc.1.t.SZC_liu_bocheng
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_liu_bocheng } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NKRsichuanmisc.1.d.SZC_pan_wenhua
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_pan_wenhua } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NKRsichuanmisc.1.d.SZC_tang_shizun
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_tang_shizun } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NKRsichuanmisc.1.d.SZC_fan_shaozeng
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_fan_shaozeng } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NKRsichuanmisc.1.d.SZC_liu_bocheng
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_liu_bocheng } }
	}


	is_triggered_only = yes #fired by on_event related to general promotions.

	trigger = {
		THIS = {
			OR = {
				is_character = SZC_pan_wenhua
				is_character = SZC_tang_shizun
				is_character = SZC_fan_shaozeng
				is_character = SZC_liu_bocheng
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanmisc.1 option NKRsichuanmisc.1.a"
		name = NKRsichuanmisc.1.a #
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_pan_wenhua } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_champion_effect_tt
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanmisc.1 option NKRsichuanmisc.1.b"
		name = NKRsichuanmisc.1.b #
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_tang_shizun } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_champion_effect_tt
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanmisc.1 option NKRsichuanmisc.1.c"
		name = NKRsichuanmisc.1.c #
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_fan_shaozeng } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_champion_effect_tt
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event NKRsichuanmisc.1 option NKRsichuanmisc.1.d"
		name = NKRsichuanmisc.1.d #
		trigger = { THIS = { is_character = SZC_liu_bocheng } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_champion_effect_tt
	}
}
